The 5 hybrid races


Bashar gives a list:

- Anu
- Vikwa (seed) desh (template) i.e. homo erectus
- Adama and Ekah
- Maz-Eh (Grays)
- Maz-Ani (Tall Grays)
Sassani
Shaya-el
Yahya-el
Shalana-ya
Enani-ka
Anu-Het
